#Intro events

country_event = { #History
	id = russia.1
	title = russia.1.t 
	desc = russia.1.d 
	picture = GFX_rus_russia_flag_event
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = { tag = RUS }
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	option = {
		name = russia.1.a
		country_event = {
			id = russia.2
			days = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.1.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		country_event = russia.1017
		country_event = {
			id = russia.2
			days = 1
		}
	}
}

			idea = rus_austerity_measures
			days = 365
		}

			country_event = {
				id = russia.4
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}

#Politics
country_event = { #Kerensky
	id = russia.5
	title = russia.5.t
	desc = russia.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_POL_assassination
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		is_puppet = no
		date > 1936.01.4
		has_country_leader = {
			ruling_only = yes
			name = "Alexandr Kerensky"
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.5.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		country_event = {
			id = russia.6
			days = 1
		}
		add_ideas = {
			rus_political_instability
		}
		add_manpower = -1
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "The Senate"
			desc = "POLITICS_SENATE_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_The_Senate.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = social_liberal_subtype
			traits = {}
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_KRSKY_DEATH
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				news_event = {
					id = worldnews.15
					days = 1
				}
			}
			RUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = worldtension.10
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	#option = { #Lives #temporarily cut
	#	name = russia.5.b
	#	ai_chance = {
	#		factor = 1
	#	}

country_event = { #Aftermath of assassination
	id = russia.6
	title = russia.6.t
	desc = russia.6.d 
	picture = GFX_report_event_RUS_Russia_Kerensky
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = russia.6.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = coalition_power
		clr_country_flag = market_liberal_coalition
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = russia.13
				days = 3
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russia.10
				days = 4
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russia.30
				days = 8
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russia.9
				days = 12
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russia.14
				days = 10
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusdem.1
				days = 6
			}
			country_event = {
				id = russia.16
				days = 30
			}
		}
		
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			elections_allowed = yes    }
		add_stability = -0.21
		set_country_flag = RUS_SEN
		parties_mp_recalc = yes
		subtract_from_variable = { senate_support = 75 }
	}
}

country_event = { #Gorgulov Trial
	id = russia.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russia.10"}
	title = russia.10.t
	desc = russia.10.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_rus_gorguloff_trial
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = russia.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_GOR_ALIVE
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_stability = -0.04
		subtract_from_variable = { senate_support = 6 }
		add_to_variable = { national_populist_mp = 20 }
		subtract_from_variable = { social_liberal_mp = 26 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Alexandr Kerensky"
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_TERROR
			set_country_flag = RUS_KER
			subtract_from_variable = { social_liberal_mp = 10 }
			load_focus_tree = RUS_KERENSKY_FOCUS
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_country_flag = RUS_KRSKY_LIVES
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_GORGULOV
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_SOLIDARISTS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_ABUKUMOV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		add_to_variable = { senate_support = 6 }
		add_to_variable = { social_democrat_mp = 10 }
		add_to_variable = { market_liberal_mp = 4 }
		add_stability = 0.04
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					ruling_only = yes
					name = "Alexandr Kerensky"
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = RUS_TERROR
			set_country_flag = RUS_KER
			load_focus_tree = RUS_KERENSKY_FOCUS
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Pardon Gorgulov?
	id = russia.11
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event.russia.11"}
	title = russia.11.t
	desc = russia.11.d
	picture = GFX_rus_gorguloff_event
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		has_country_flag = RUS_SAVI
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Boris Savinkov"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_country_flag = RUS_GOR_ALIVE
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russia.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_post_assassination
					option = RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_KORNILOV_SAVINKOV
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = russia.12
				days = 20
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russia.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_GORGULOV
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_SOLIDARISTS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_ABUKUMOV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		add_political_power = -25
	}
	
}

country_event = { #Power Struggle
	id = russia.28
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event.russia.28"}
	title = russia.28.t
	desc = russia.28.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = russia.28.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_SOLIDARISTS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_ABUKUMOV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_populist
			long_name = RUS_gorgulov_party_long
			name = RUS_gorgulov_party
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			RUS_Pavel_T_Gorgulov_hog_npo
			RUS_Ivan_Kolesnikov_for_npo
			RUS_Aleksandr_Antonov_eco_npo
			RUS_Pyotr_Tokmakov_sec_npo
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_SAVI
		set_country_flag = RUS_GORGULOV

		set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_GOR

	}

		}
		}		
	}

			}
		}

		}

			popularity = 0.1

			popularity = 0.1
			}

				id = rusd.25
				days = 2
			}

				RUS_Aleksey_A_Ignatiev_for_pau
				RUS_Ivan_P_Romanovskiy_eco_pau
				RUS_Aleksandr_P_Balk_sec_pau 
			}
			load_focus_tree = russia_focus
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = rusd.999 #Hidden event to fire unrest events
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_idea = rus_political_instability
			has_idea = rus_political_instability1
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusd.999"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusd.999
				days = 15
				random = 600
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Political Murder
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_political_murder }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = RUS_political_murder days = 50 value = 1 }
		country_event = rusd.1
	}
	option = { #Bombing
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_political_bombing }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = RUS_political_bombing days = 50 value = 1 }
		country_event = rusd.3
	}
	option = { #Peasant unrest
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_peasant_unrest }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = RUS_peasant_unrest days = 50 value = 1 }
		country_event = rusd.4
	}
	option = { #Agitation in the countryside
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_agitation }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = RUS_agitation days = 50 value = 1 }
		country_event = rusd.5
	}
	option = { #Workers' demonstration
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_demonstration }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 3
		}
		set_country_flag = { flag = RUS_demonstration days = 50 value = 1 }
		country_event = rusd.7
	}
	option = { #Workers' strike
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = rus_fulfilled_strike
				has_idea = rus_minor_strike
				has_country_flag = RUS_disable_minor_strikes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
		country_event = rusd.8
	}
	option = { #General strike
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_idea = rus_general_strike
				has_idea = rus_general_strike_big
				has_idea = rus_fulfilled_strike_general
				has_idea = rus_fulfilled_strike_general_malus
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		country_event = rusd.13
	}
	option = { #nothing
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 7
		}
	}
}

		days = 2

				has_government = radical_socialist
			}
		}

			factor = 25

		if = {

					has_government = syndicalist

				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { senate_support = 50 }
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialist

			}
			NOT = {

###Duma Decisions
country_event = { #PLSR plan
	id = rusdem.10
	title = rusdem.10.t
	desc = rusdem.10.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rusdem.10.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = {
					var = mp_support
					value = 275
					compare = less_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = senate_support
					value = 75
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = voting_unlikely
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusdem.11
				days = 1
			}
		}
		
	}
	option = {
		name = rusdem.10.a
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					var = mp_support
					value = 275
					compare = greater_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = senate_support
					value = 75
					compare = greater_than
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = voting_likely
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusdem.12
				days = 1
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = plsr_plan_accepted
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = radical_socialist_mp
					value = 23
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = NSP_MIN_30
			subtract_from_variable = { radical_socialist_mp = 23 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = social_democrat_mp
					value = 30
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RSDRP_MIN_30
			subtract_from_variable = { social_democrat_mp = 30 }
		}
		mp_support_calc = yes
	}
}

		add_political_power = -25
	}

		if = {

					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = PLSR_MIN_25
			subtract_from_variable = { syndicalist_mp = 21 }
		}
		mp_support_calc = yes
	}

			}
		}
		set_country_flag = monarchy_referendum_accepted

		}

	}

		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_select_denikin
		set_country_flag = RUS_selectdenikin
		add_ideas = RUS_rovs_denikin
		set_variable = { var = RUS.denikin_influence value = 10 }
		set_variable = { var = RUS.wrangel_influence value = 5 }
	}
	option = {
		name = rusd.209.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 10000
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = RUS_post_assassination
					option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_KORNILOV
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_selectwrangel
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_select_wrangel
		add_ideas = RUS_rovs_wrangel
		set_variable = { var = RUS.denikin_influence value = 5 }
		set_variable = { var = RUS.wrangel_influence value = 10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = rusd.209.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 10000
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_KORNILOV_SAVINKOV
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_GORGULOV
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_SOLIDARISTS
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = RUS_post_assassination
						option = RULE_OPTION_RUS_POST_ASSASSINATION_ABUKUMOV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_selectsavinkov
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_select_savinkov
	}
}

		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

		name = rusd.210.a

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_selectdenikin

				}
				random_list = {
					90 = {
						country_event = {
							id = rusd.212
							days = 2
						}
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = {
							id = rusd.211
							days = 2
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_selectwrangel
					check_variable = { RUS.wrangel_influence > 6 }
				}
				random_list = {
					90 = {
						country_event = {
							id = rusd.212
							days = 2
						}
					}
					10 = {
						country_event = {
							id = rusd.211
							days = 2
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_selectdenikin
					check_variable = { RUS.denikin_influence < 7 }
				}
				random_list = {
					30 = {
						country_event = {
							id = rusd.212
							days = 2
						}
					}
					70 = {
						country_event = {
							id = rusd.211
							days = 2
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_selectwrangel
					check_variable = { RUS.wrangel_influence < 7 }
				}
				random_list = {
					40 = {
						country_event = {
							id = rusd.212
							days = 2
						}
					}
					60 = {
						country_event = {
							id = rusd.211
							days = 2
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = rusd.162.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = rusd.162.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_republic_rig
					has_country_flag = RUS_monarchy_rig
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_referendum_is_rigged
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_republic_rig
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_monarchy_rig
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = RUS_monarchy_sympathies
						value > 4
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_monarchy_guaranteed
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_monarchy_rig
				}
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_republic_rig
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = RUS_monarchy_sympathies
						value < -4
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_republic_guaranteed
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = RUS_monarchy_sympathies
					value > 2
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_monarchy_likely
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = {
					flag = RUS_monarchy_sympathies
					value < -1
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_republic_likely
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusd.163
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 0
		}
		add_ideas = RUS_increased_zemstvo_investment
		RUS_zemstvo_focus_events = yes
	}

		name = rusd.172.c

			num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 1
		}
		add_ideas = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment
		RUS_zemstvo_focus_events = yes
	}
}

	### Effects

	is_triggered_only = yes

	#SOCIAL
	option = { #new hospitals
		name = rusd.174.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_hospital
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure }
		}
		RUS_calculate_zemstva_variables = yes
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = 0.001 }
		add_stability = RUS_zemstvo_base_value
		RUS_clear_zemstvo_data = yes
	}

	option = { #new schools
		name = rusd.174.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_schools
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure }
		}
		RUS_calculate_zemstva_variables = yes
		add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = 25 }
		add_political_power = RUS_zemstvo_base_value
		RUS_clear_zemstvo_data = yes
	}

	option = { #housing programme
		name = rusd.174.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_housing
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure }
		}
		RUS_calculate_zemstva_variables = yes
		multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = 0.001 }
		add_war_support = RUS_zemstvo_base_value
		RUS_clear_zemstvo_data = yes
	}

	option = { #failed civil investments
		name = rusd.174.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_hospital
				has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_housing
				has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_schools
			}
			has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure
		}
		RUS_calculate_zemstva_variables = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_hospital }
			multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = -0.001 }
			add_stability = RUS_zemstvo_base_value
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_housing }
			multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = -0.001 }
			add_war_support = RUS_zemstvo_base_value
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_schools }
			add_to_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = 25 }
			multiply_temp_variable = { RUS_zemstvo_base_value = -1 }
			add_political_power = RUS_zemstvo_base_value
		}
		RUS_clear_zemstvo_data = yes
	}

		name = rusd.174.a

			has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_synthetics
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure }
		}
		event_target:RUS_zemstvo_state_1 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = synthetic_refinery
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		RUS_clear_zemstvo_data = yes
	}

	option = { #failed industrial investment
		name = rusd.174.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_civilian_industry
				has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_military_industry
				has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_infrastructure
				has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_agriculture
				has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_synthetics
			}
			has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = RUS_zemstva_bad_investment
				days = 180
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_increased_zemstvo_investment }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = RUS_zemstva_bad_investment
				days = 120
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = RUS_zemstva_bad_investment
				days = 60
			}
		}
		RUS_clear_zemstvo_data = yes
	}

	#RESEARCH 

	option = { #industrial research advance
		name = rusd.174.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_industry_research
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure }
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_industry_research
		if = { # big investment
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_large_zemstvo_investment }
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = RUS_zemsvto_research
				bonus = 0.6
				uses = 1
				category = industry
				category = electronics
			}
		}
		else_if = { # medium investment
			limit = { has_idea = RUS_increased_zemstvo_investment }
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = RUS_zemsvto_research
				bonus = 0.4
				uses = 1
				category = industry
				category = electronics
			}
		}
		else = { # small investment
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = RUS_zemsvto_research
				bonus = 0.2
				uses = 1
				category = industry
				category = electronics
			}
		}
		RUS_clear_zemstvo_data = yes
	}

	option = { #industrial research breakthrough
		name = rusd.174.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_industry_research_bonus
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_zemstvo_failure }

		}

							days = 2

							days = 2
						}
					}

							days = 2
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

				has_country_flag = plsr_support_frunze
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SOV_zinoviev_plsr_is_not_guaranteed
			hidden_effect = {

country_event = { #voroshilov plot
	id = russoc.63
	title = russoc.63.t
	desc = russoc.63.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = russoc.63.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = RUS_Georgiy_K_Zhukov_hog_tot
			}
			remove_ideas = RUS_Georgiy_K_Zhukov_hog_tot
		}
		set_country_flag = Georgiy_K_Zhukov_dead
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 457 }
			retire = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					Tukha_Influence > Frunze_Influence
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mikhail Tukhachevsky"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Mikhail_Tukhachevskiy.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = totalist_subtype
				traits = { red_napoleon }
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mikhail Frunze"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Mikhail_Frunze.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = totalist_subtype
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = Zhukov_Influence
			value = 0
		}
	}
}

				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = Mikhail_Tukhachevskiy_dead
						has_country_flag = zinoviev_supported_tukha
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = plsr_will_support_tukha
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = russoc.70
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = Mikhail_Tukhachevskiy_dead
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = plsr_will_support_zhukov
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = russoc.69
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = plsr_will_support_tukha
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = russoc.71
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russoc.68.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		set_country_flag = tu_with_limited_state_control
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = Mikhail_Tukhachevskiy_dead
						has_country_flag = zinoviev_supported_zhukov
						NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Frunze_dead }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = Georgiy_K_Zhukov_dead
						has_country_flag = zinoviev_supported_tukha
						NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Frunze_dead }
					}					
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = plsr_will_support_frunze
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = russoc.71
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = Mikhail_Tukhachevskiy_dead
						has_country_flag = zinoviev_supported_frunze
						NOT = { has_country_flag = Georgiy_K_Zhukov_dead }
					}
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = Mikhail_Frunze_dead
						has_country_flag = zinoviev_supported_tukha
						NOT = { has_country_flag = Georgiy_K_Zhukov_dead }
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = plsr_will_support_zhukov
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = russoc.69
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {

						has_country_flag = zinoviev_supported_tukha

			}

		}

			limit = {
				has_country_flag = state_controlled_tu
			}

		}

			popularity = 0.2
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = Zhukov_Influence
			value = 25
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Troika dissolves
	id = russoc.85
	immediate = { set_country_flag = SOV_Troika_dissolved }
	title = russoc.85.t
	desc = russoc.85.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = russoc.85.a
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					var = Zhukov_Influence
					value = Tukha_Influence
					compare = greater_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = Zhukov_Influence
					value = Frunze_Influence
					compare = greater_than
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = Georgiy_K_Zhukov_dead }
			}
		}			
		set_country_flag = zhukov_rules_alone
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = RUS_red_army_party_long
			name = RUS_red_army_party
		}
		clr_country_flag = SOV_Troika_power_struggle
	}
	option = {
		name = russoc.85.b
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					var = Tukha_Influence
					value = Zhukov_Influence
					compare = greater_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = Tukha_Influence
					value = Frunze_Influence
					compare = greater_than
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Tukhachevskiy_dead }
			}
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mikhail Tukhachevsky"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Mikhail_Tukhachevskiy.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = red_junta_subtype
			traits = { red_napoleon }
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = SOV_tukhachevsky
		set_country_flag = tukhachevsky_power
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = SOV_tukh_party_long
			name = SOV_tukh_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = zinoviev_supported_tukha
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = RUS_Grigoriy_Y_Zinoviev_hog_tot
		}
		clr_country_flag = SOV_Troika_power_struggle
	}
	option = {
		name = russoc.85.c
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					var = Frunze_Influence
					value = Tukha_Influence
					compare = greater_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = Frunze_Influence
					value = Zhukov_Influence
					compare = greater_than
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Frunze_dead }
			}
		}			
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Mikhail Frunze"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Mikhail_Frunze.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = red_junta_subtype
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = SOV_tukhachevsky
		set_country_flag = tukhachevsky_power
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = SOV_frunze_party_long
			name = SOV_frunze_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = zinoviev_supported_frunze
			}
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = RUS_Grigoriy_Y_Zinoviev_hog_tot
		}
		clr_country_flag = SOV_Troika_power_struggle
	}
}

						id = russoc.119
						days = 2
						random = 48
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = MTR
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						tag = AZE
						has_war = no
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction = no
					}
					country_event = {
						id = russoc.119
						days = 2
						random = 48
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = russoc.119.c #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				tag = POL
				has_dictatorship_government = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = rusfor.11.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rusfor.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_subject_of = RUS
			}			
		}
		set_country_flag = psc_council_vote
		add_to_array = { global.PSC_voters = ROOT }
		add_political_power = 25
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.12
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rusfor.11.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.13
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

		set_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent

country_event = { #PS - Czechoslovakia Result
	id = rusfor.27
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.27" }
	title = rusfor.27.t
	desc = rusfor.27.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = rusfor.27.a
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent
			set_country_flag = czechoslovakia_independent_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_separate_independent
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_separate_independent
			set_country_flag = czechoslovakia_separate_approved
		}
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = rusfor.27.b
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_independent
		clr_global_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_separate_independent
		set_country_flag = PSC_czechoslovakia_denied
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Panslavic Congress - Galicia
	id = rusfor.22
	title = rusfor.22.t
	desc = rusfor.22.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		AND = {
			RUS = {
				has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			}
			OR = {
				UKR = {
					has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
				}
				GAL = {
					has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
				}
				POL = {
					has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
				}
				AUS = {
					has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rusfor.22.a
		trigger = {
			country_exists = POL
			country_exists = UKR
			UKR = {
				has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			}
			POL = {
				has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}		
		activate_mission = PSC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
		set_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = rusfor.26
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = rusfor.31
			days = 15
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rusfor.22.b
		trigger = {
			country_exists = POL
			NOT = { country_exists = UKR }
			POL = {
				has_country_flag = psc_council_vote
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}		
		activate_mission = PSC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
		set_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = rusfor.26
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = rusfor.31
			days = 15
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = rusfor.22.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {country_exists = POL }
			10 = {
				owner = {
					tag = RUS
				}
			}
			NOT = { country_exists = UKR }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		activate_mission = PSC_vote_timer
		set_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
		set_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				country_event = rusfor.26
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = rusfor.31
			days = 15
		}
	}

	id = rusfor.31
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.31" }
	title = rusfor.31.t
	desc = rusfor.31.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy4
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {	#Approved!
		name = rusfor.27.a
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
			set_country_flag = galicia_split_ukraine_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
			set_country_flag = galicia_split_russia_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
			set_country_flag = galicia_annex_russia_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
			set_country_flag = eastgalicia_split_approved
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_ukraine
			}
			clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_ukraine
			set_country_flag = eastgalicia_ukraine_approved
		}
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > 0 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {	#Denied!
		name = rusfor.27.b
		clear_variable = global.psc_yes_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_no_votes
		clear_variable = global.psc_abstain_votes
		clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_ukraine
		clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_ukraine
		clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_split_russia
		clr_global_flag = PSC_galicia_annex_russia
		clr_global_flag = PSC_eastgalicia_split
		clr_global_flag = psc_vote_ongoing
		for_each_scope_loop = {
			array = global.PSC_voters
			THIS = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
					}
					clr_country_flag = PSC_we_voted_this_time
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { global.psc_yes_votes > global.psc_no_votes }
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Free Czechoslovakia
	id = rusfor.1305
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1305" }
	title = rusfor.1305.t
	desc = rusfor.1305.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rusfor.1305.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = czechoslovakia_independent_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CZE
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			CZE = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Johann II zu Schwarzenberg"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						has_country_flag = CZE_SVK_was_puppeted
						}
					}
				}
			set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_czechoslavakia
			
			leave_faction = yes
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = czechoslovakia_separate_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CZE
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CZE
				}
					CZE = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			CZE = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Johann II zu Schwarzenberg"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							has_country_flag = CZE_SVK_was_puppeted
							}
						}
					}
				
				leave_faction = yes
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SVK = { is_subject_of = AUS }
				}
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = SVK
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
				SVK = { 
					leave_faction = yes
					separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						SVK = { NOT = { owns_state = 664 } }
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = 664
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				AUS = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = SVK
						}
					}

country_event = { #Russia agrees
	id = rusfor.1310
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1310" }
	title = rusfor.1310.t
	desc = rusfor.1310.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = rusfor.1310.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = czechoslovakia_independent_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CZE
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SVK
						is_core_of = CZE
					}
				}
				CZE = {
					transfer_state = PREV
					add_state_core = PREV
				}
				}
			}
			CZE = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Johann II zu Schwarzenberg"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						has_country_flag = CZE_SVK_was_puppeted
						}
					}
				}
			set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_czechoslavakia
			
			leave_faction = yes
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = czechoslovakia_separate_approved }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CZE = { is_subject_of = AUS } }
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = CZE
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			AUS = {
				every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CZE
				}
					CZE = {
						transfer_state = PREV
						add_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			CZE = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_country_leader = {
									name = "Johann II zu Schwarzenberg"
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							has_country_flag = CZE_SVK_was_puppeted
							}
						}
					}
				
				separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SVK = { is_subject_of = AUS }
				}
				AUS = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = SVK
						autonomous_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						SVK = {
							NOT = { 
							owns_state = 1122
							owns_state = 1136
							}
						} 
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = 1122
						transfer_state = 1136
					}
				}
				SVK = { 
					leave_faction = yes
					separate_peace_all_wars = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				AUS = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = SVK
						}
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
				HUN = {
					every_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							is_core_of = SVK
						}
					}
					SVK = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = zakarpatie_cze_approved }
			}
			CZE = {
				transfer_state = 73
				transfer_state = 1119
				add_state_core = 73
				add_state_core = 1119
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = { has_country_flag = zakarpatie_slo_approved }
			}
			SVK = {
				transfer_state = 73
				transfer_state = 1119
				add_state_core = 73
				add_state_core = 1119
			}
		}
		transfer_state = 69
		transfer_state = 71
		transfer_state = 74
		transfer_state = 786
		transfer_state = 1133
		transfer_state = 1138
		transfer_state = 1139
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = CZE
			relation = military_access
			active = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1001" }
	title = rusfor.1001.t
	desc = rusfor.1001.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1001.a #Accept
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				don_is_pro_russian = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				kuban_is_pro_russian = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1002
				days = 1
				random = 24
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = DKB }
				every_country = { #GEO & AZR
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = KUB
							tag = DKB
							tag = KLY
							tag = MTR
							tag = GEO
							tag = AZE
						}
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						has_war = no
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction = no
					}
					country_event = {
						id = rusfor.1001
						days = 2
						random = 48
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1001.b #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1019" }
	title = rusfor.1019.t
	desc = rusfor.1019.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1019.a #Perhaps we have to overthrow Cossack rule over Don-Kuban.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		DKB = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1015
				days = 5
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1019.b #It means war!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				DKB = { is_guaranteed_by = GER }
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = DKB
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Baku Oil Fields
	id = rusfor.1020
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1020" }
	title = rusfor.1020.t
	desc = rusfor.1020.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1020.a #Take over the Baku Oil Concern and control their Government!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = -150
		send_equipment = {
			target = AZE
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 2000
		}
		AZE = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1021
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1020.b #Guarantee the security of Azerbaijan and invest in the oil fields.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		give_guarantee = AZE
		AZE = {
			every_owned_state = { remove_claim_by = ROOT }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1276
				days = 125
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rusfor.1020.c #Who built Baku's oil plants? Make plans for a hostile takeover!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = 3 
			name = rusfor.1020.t
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AZE 
			modifier = KR_outraged
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything 
			target = AZE
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rusfor.1020.e #We shall take back our stolen plants by force, right now!
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Realpolitik }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AZE = { 
					OR = {
						is_in_faction = yes 
						is_guaranteed_by = GER
						is_subject = yes
					}
				}
			}				
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = AZE 
			type = annex_everything
		}
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = 3 
			name = rusfor.1020.t
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Russian Investment AZE
	id = rusfor.1021
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1021" }
	title = rusfor.1021.t
	desc = rusfor.1021.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1021.a #Invite the Russians to protect and develop Azerbaijan.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1023
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				send_equipment = {
					target = AZE
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = 2000
				}
			}
		}
		990 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
			add_building_construction = {
				type = arms_factory
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	} 

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1021.b #Decline the offer, attempt to limit Russian influence!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1022
				days = 2
				random = 48
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = rusfor.1048
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1048" }
	title = rusfor.1048.t
	desc = rusfor.1048.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1048.a #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
		}
		FROM = {
			clr_country_flag = RUS_GER_blocks_caucasus
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					is_guaranteed_by = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						region = 134 #Caucasus
						region = 135 #Kuban
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = PREV
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = PREV
					relation = military_access
					active = no
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
			country_event = rusfor.1050
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1053
					days = 1
					random = 24
				}
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1054
					days = 2
					random = 48
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1048.b #Never!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1049

			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_subject = ARM
					has_subject = GEO
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 20
		transfer_state = 1000
		transfer_state = 1001
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1072.b #Give the land to our puppets!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_subject = ARM
				has_subject = GEO
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 20
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_subject = ARM
			}
			ARM = { transfer_state = 1000 }
			remove_state_claim = 1000
		}
		else = {
			transfer_state = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_subject = GEO
			}
			GEO = { transfer_state = 1001 }
			remove_state_claim = 1001
		}
		else = {
			transfer_state = 1001
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Crush Transamur
	id = rusfor.1082
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1082" }
	title = rusfor.1082.t
	desc = rusfor.1082.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1082.a #all Russians must be under Russian rule! claim TRM
		if = {
			limit = {
				TRM = {
					OR = {
					is_subject_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism }
				JAP = {
					country_event = {
						id = rusfor.1084
						days = 2
						random = 48
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				JAP = {
					country_event = {
						id = rusfor.1083
						days = 2
						random = 48
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				TRM = {
					NOT = { is_in_faction_with = JAP }
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			TRM = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.10877
					days = 2
					random = 48
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = TRM
				type = annex_everything
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						country_exists = YAK
						country_exists = BRY
						country_exists = SIB
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					country_event = {
						id = rusfor.10820
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = TRM }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #We've been defeated! FIN
	id = rusfor.1232
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1232" }
	title = {
		text = rusfor.1232.t.victory
		trigger = {
			NOT = { surrender_progress > 0.2 }	
		}
	}
	title = {
		text = rusfor.1232.defeat
		trigger = {
			surrender_progress > 0.2	
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rusfor.1232.d.defeat
		trigger = { surrender_progress > 0.2 }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rusfor.1232.d.victory
		trigger = {
			NOT = { surrender_progress > 0.2 }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = FIN
		has_war_with = 219.owner
		is_valid_peace_target = yes
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_enemy_tag = 219.owner }
		var:RUS_enemy_tag = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
			is_valid_peace_target = yes
		}
		OR = {
			#Finland loses
			surrender_progress > 0.2
			#Finland wins
			var:RUS_enemy_tag = { surrender_progress > 0.1 }
			controls_state = 195 #Petrograd
			AND = {
				controls_state = 213 #Murmansk
				controls_state = 215 #Kem
				controls_state = 216 #Petrozavodsk
				controls_state = 722 #Petsamo
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_FIN_offered_peace }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = { flag = RUS_FIN_offered_peace days = 90 value = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { surrender_progress > 0.2 }
			}
			set_global_flag = { flag = RUS_defeated_by_FIN days = 60 value = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1232.a #Sue for peace!
		var:219.owner = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1233
				days = 1
				random = 24
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1232.b #We can still win this!
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
}

country_event = { #ROM-RUS peace deal
	id = rusfor.1236
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1236" }
	title = rusfor.1236.t
	
	title = {
		text = rusfor.1236.t.victory
		trigger = { has_global_flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rusfor.1236.d.victory
		trigger = { has_global_flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM }
	}
	
	title = {
		text = rusfor.1236.t.defeat
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rusfor.1236.d.defeat
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ROM
		has_war_with = 219.owner
		owns_state = 78
		owns_state = 1222
		is_valid_peace_target = yes
		set_temp_variable = { RUS_enemy_tag = 219.owner }
		var:RUS_enemy_tag = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
			is_valid_peace_target = yes
		}
		OR = {
			#Romania loses
			var:RUS_enemy_tag = {
				controls_state = 78 #Bessarabia
				controls_state = 1222 # Bujak
				controls_state = 79 #Moldavia
			}
			surrender_progress > 0.15
			#Romania wins
			var:RUS_enemy_tag = { surrender_progress > 0.1 }
			controls_state = 202 #Kiev
			controls_state = 226 #Ekaterinoslav
			AND = {
				controls_state = 192 #Odessa
				controls_state = 791 #Podolia
				OR = {
					controls_state = 197 #Kherson
					controls_state = 198 #Vinnitsa
					controls_state = 199 #Proskurov
					controls_state = 203 #Cherkasy
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_ROM_offered_peace }
	}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = { flag = RUS_ROM_offered_peace days = 90 value = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					surrender_progress > 0.15
					NOT = { controls_state = 78 }
				}
			}
			set_global_flag = { flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM days = 60 value = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1236.a #We have no choice; send word to Moscow.
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM }
		}
		var:219.owner = {
			country_event = { id = rusfor.1237 days = 1 random = 24 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1236.b #We can still win this!
		trigger = {

	title = rusfor.1238.t

	desc = {
		text = rusfor.1238.d.victory
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rusfor.1238.d.defeat
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM }
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1238.a #United just to be torn asunder again...
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = FROM
					is_claimed_by = FROM
					state = 78 #Bessarabia
					state = 1222
					if = {
						limit = {
							FROM = { owns_state = 89 } #Stanislawow
						}
						state = 80 #Cernauti
					}
				}
			}
			FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		FROM = {
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rusfor.1238.b 
		trigger = { has_global_flag = RUS_defeated_by_ROM }
		FROM = {
			remove_state_claim = 78 #Bessarabia
			remove_state_claim = 1222
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FROM
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
	}
}

	id = rusfor.1422
	title = rusfor.1422.t
	desc = rusfor.1422.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = RUS
			tag = SOV
		}
		controls_state = 408
		has_war_with = TRM
	}
	option = {
		name = rusfor.1422.a
		remove_ideas = RUS_Siberian_War_Buff
		TRM = { separate_peace_all_wars = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				TRM = { is_subject_of = JAP }
			}
			white_peace = JAP
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = TRM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}		
	}
	option = {
		name = rusfor.1422.b
		trigger = {
			TRM = { is_subject_of = JAP }
		}
		remove_ideas = RUS_Siberian_War_Buff
		TRM = { separate_peace_all_wars = yes }
		annex_country = {
			target = TRM
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = JAP
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
	}
}

				is_in_asia = yes
			}
			event_target:peace_country = { white_peace = PREV }
		}
		JAP = { transfer_state = 408 }
		JAP = { transfer_state = 409 }
		JAP = { transfer_state = 637 }
		JAP = { transfer_state = 562 }
		637 = { add_claim_by = JAP }
		562 = { add_claim_by = JAP }
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_chinese_tag = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT

		}
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes

			days = 900
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
	}
}
